      <div style="right:0" class="readable stacked" id="description">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer15305646693020867832">Dr. Matthew Hiller is about to face the most difficult moment of his life. The brilliant neurosurgeon's next case is not simply a suffering patient for whom he is the last hope. It is Silvia - his only love. Now married to one of the richest men in the world, Silvia can still evoke the same feelings in him that she did so long ago. Even after all this time, he has not reco</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText15305646693020867832">Dr. Matthew Hiller is about to face the most difficult moment of his life. The brilliant neurosurgeon's next case is not simply a suffering patient for whom he is the last hope. It is Silvia - his only love. Now married to one of the richest men in the world, Silvia can still evoke the same feelings in him that she did so long ago. Even after all this time, he has not recovered from her unexplained disappearance on the eve of their marriage - and thoughts of her have haunted him ever since. As a doctor, he must try to help her. As a spurned lover - and a married man - he must try to forget the past. And he dares not think about what might happen if he actually succeeds in saving her life...</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="15305646693020867832">...more</a>

              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer226966891">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17993313935238791499"> I love to read Erich Segal books. I just love the way he puts words together. This book is the story of two doctors that go to Africa in the 70s and fall in love. Then they break up unexpectedly. Now, twenty years later the female has a brain tumor and the man (now Dr.) must operate. They do not particularly have a good reunion from the man's point of view. But it does set him free. I really enjoyed this book.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review nosyndicate" id="review_81507570">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/81507570?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Mar 29, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/3048260-erin-paperbackstash-book-hoarders-unite" class="user" title="Erin (Paperbackstash) *Book Hoarders Unite!*">Erin (Paperbackstash) *Book Hoarders Unite!*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>



        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/3048260-erin-paperbackstash-book-hoarders-unite?shelf=a-own-book-form" class="actionLinkLite">a-own-book-form</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/3048260-erin-paperbackstash-book-hoarders-unite?shelf=drama-gen-fiction" class="actionLinkLite">drama-gen-fiction</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/3048260-erin-paperbackstash-book-hoarders-unite?shelf=3-star" class="actionLinkLite">3-star</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/3048260-erin-paperbackstash-book-hoarders-unite?shelf=reviewed" class="actionLinkLite">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer81507570">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14033964709950623023">It's tempting to say it's a romance, but it's really not.<br /><br />It's a drama which entires its story upon a romantic relationship.<br /><br />It's unusual for the biggest strength of a good book to be amazing writing. I can't think of many books that stand out in the memory as so well written, so imaginatively poised. Segal is an author I need to find again, for his way of melding words inspires. Easy to follow but beautiful at the same time, his poise is almost poetic, but it's not cloying.<br /><br />Plot-wise it's interest</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText14033964709950623023">It's tempting to say it's a romance, but it's really not.<br /><br />It's a drama which entires its story upon a romantic relationship.<br /><br />It's unusual for the biggest strength of a good book to be amazing writing. I can't think of many books that stand out in the memory as so well written, so imaginatively poised. Segal is an author I need to find again, for his way of melding words inspires. Easy to follow but beautiful at the same time, his poise is almost poetic, but it's not cloying.<br /><br />Plot-wise it's interesting and I don't think I've read one like this one before - not overly romantic, not terribly suspenseful or gripping, and the story wraps up with a sad note (but not a haunting one.) Basically a doctor meets a patient of his who is dying, and recognizes the woman as a life of his life, and then begins remembering their relationship twenty years ago. A mixed bag here. Sometimes I did get a bit bored with some of the backstory details. Even if it's not overly nail-biting, there's something about it that keeps you reading.<br /><br />The protagonist is a sympathetic character, a man with morals and drive but with human flaw. It was cool to read this kind of story from a male perspective.The heroine is likeable but of course from the protagonists POV twenty years later she is at fault. The ending allows him to feel closure for a life of his life.<br /><br />It's not a novel that will grip your heart, but the magic of the writer at least makes your heart feel it.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="14033964709950623023">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <a href="/user/show/27388905-pallavi-soni" class="user" title="Pallavi Soni">Pallavi Soni</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok">it was ok</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1497822592">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13041057901763350126">A short love story of Silvia and Matthew, hailing from completely different social background and brought together by their affection for music. Two lovers vowed to spend their life together only to fall apart in pieces.<br /><br />This is the second book I have read that is written by Erich Segal. Love Story was brilliant in its portrayal of evident and non-evident emotions. Only Love, throughout its length was also impeccable, the everlasting bond between Matthew and Evie and the magnetism between Matthew</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText13041057901763350126">A short love story of Silvia and Matthew, hailing from completely different social background and brought together by their affection for music. Two lovers vowed to spend their life together only to fall apart in pieces.<br /><br />This is the second book I have read that is written by Erich Segal. Love Story was brilliant in its portrayal of evident and non-evident emotions. Only Love, throughout its length was also impeccable, the everlasting bond between Matthew and Evie and the magnetism between Matthew and Silvia. A heartbreaking story of a love lost and a love found. But when it comes to end, how he (Matthew) can say that I have always loved you, Evie. We, as human, always keep parts of them whom we loved once. One can be free and moved on. And in order to do so, we forgive them and ourselves, keep the good memories with ourselves and not put blame on the other one. Whatever the reason Silvia had for her disappearance from his life whether it was sense of responsibility or fear for survival, it cannot change the fact what she and Matthew had once was beautiful and it was Love.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="13041057901763350126">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12383391444865402397">This novel is my first encounter with Erich Segal's work. "Love Story" and "Oliver's Story" are maybe the more popular books, but for me this one surely amongst the best of Segal's<br /><br />It was from a long time ago, around my last years in college. This book really impressed me, and successfully dragged me on through several other works of erich segal such as The Class, Prizes, The Doctors, Man Woman and Child, Love Story, and Oliver's Story.<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9727183129604563663"><p>Kutipan Favorit : Ia tersenyum padaku, dan senyumnya menghancurkan seluruh reaksi autoimunitas-ku untuk sungguh-sungguh jatuh cinta kepadanya. (Halaman 35)</p><p> <br /><br /></p><p>Only Love adalah buku pertama karya beliau yang saya baca. Dengan alur yang dibuat maju-mundur, cerita dituturkan dengan menarik, cepat dan cerdas sehingga tidak membosankan saat membacanya. Dari karakter-karakter tokohnya, penulis seolah ingin menyampaikan banyak pesan-pesan kehidupan.</p><p> <br /><br /></p><p>Selain ukuran font-nya yang saya rasakan bikin sakit mat</p></span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9727183129604563663"><p>Kutipan Favorit : Ia tersenyum padaku, dan senyumnya menghancurkan seluruh reaksi autoimunitas-ku untuk sungguh-sungguh jatuh cinta kepadanya. (Halaman 35)</p><p>
  <br /><br /></p><p>Only Love adalah buku pertama karya beliau yang saya baca. Dengan alur yang dibuat maju-mundur, cerita dituturkan dengan menarik, cepat dan cerdas sehingga tidak membosankan saat membacanya. Dari karakter-karakter tokohnya, penulis seolah ingin menyampaikan banyak pesan-pesan kehidupan.</p><p>
  <br /><br /></p><p>Selain ukuran font-nya yang saya rasakan bikin sakit mata karena kecil-kecil. Tapi, itu bisa dimaklumi karena dimensi bukunya pun memang kecil. Secara keseluruhan, hampir tidak ada kekurangan yang saya rasakan untuk buku ini.</p><p>
  <br /><br /></p><p>Review saya selengkapnya : <a rel="nofollow" href="http://deebacalah.blogspot.com/2015/08/book-review-only-love-by-erich-segal.html" target="_blank">http://deebacalah.blogspot.com/2015/0...</a></p><p>

<span id="freeTextContainer18131554767338397971">I read this back when I was about 14 and thought it was so romantic. It also inspired me to want to someday do one of those medical missions to a third-world country.<br />So I thought it might be fun to read it as an adult. It wasn't quite so impressive this time around. This compelling, all-consuming love wasn't based on anything, just on that intangible, inexpressible SOMETHING that happens when you're soul mates. That irritates me. And then I didn't feel satisfied with how it ended. <br />So if you're l</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText18131554767338397971">I read this back when I was about 14 and thought it was so romantic. It also inspired me to want to someday do one of those medical missions to a third-world country.<br />So I thought it might be fun to read it as an adult. It wasn't quite so impressive this time around. This compelling, all-consuming love wasn't based on anything, just on that intangible, inexpressible SOMETHING that happens when you're soul mates. That irritates me. And then I didn't feel satisfied with how it ended. <br />So if you're looking for a realistic look at love, this isn't the book for you. But if you just want to read something romantic, this might fit the bill.<br />P.S. I have no qualifications to do one of those medical missions. Oh well. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5840986451410740028">Those of you who know me most likely also know that I am at best ambivalent about romance novels and at worst find them atrocious. Even so, Only Love is an enjoyable, quick, fairly tasteful bubblegum book. It does not provide much depth, as far as probing the human heart, but Segal has his moments of insight. Aside from the infernal love of fragments that so many modern authors share, the writing is decent.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/gcHAx3oiRUGVKa5EymqJvbyU+K6WiYDFVBj3OM2HRKb0zjQ7zqd74qM0gJtSEyUvwWQ+/OHYal/WWZOL6PrVw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/15516.Erich_Segal">About Erich Segal</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/15516.Erich_Segal"><img alt="15516" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1202419115p2/15516.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer15868101718183076595">Erich Wolf Segal was an American author, screenwriter, and educator. He was best-known for writing the novel <em>Love Story</em>, a bestseller, and writing the motion picture of the same name, which was a major hit.</span>

    </div>
    <a href="/author/show/15516.Erich_Segal" class="actionLink moreLink">More about Erich Segal...</a>
<div class="clear"></div></div></div><div class="bigBoxBottom"></div></div>


    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/list/15516.Erich_Segal">Books by Erich Segal</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
    <div data-current-user-id="false" data-use-wtr-tooltip="true" class="js-dataTooltip">
        <div data-placement="bottom-left" data-resource-id="73968" data-resource-type="Book" class="js-tooltipTrigger tooltipTrigger">
          <a href="/book/show/73968.Love_Story"><img width="50" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/books/1388812297m/73968.jpg" id="more_book_73968" /></a>
